 <script type="text/javascript">
  //&lt;![CDATA[

// Set cookie
function setCookie(name, value, expires, path, domain, secure) {
document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) +
((expires == null) ? "" : "; expires=" + expires.toGMTString()) +
((path == null) ? "" : "; path=" + path) +
((domain == null) ? "" : "; domain=" + domain) +
((secure == null) ? "" : "; secure");
}

// Read cookie
function getCookie(name){
var cname = name + "=";
var dc = document.cookie;
if (dc.length &gt; 0) {
begin = dc.indexOf(cname);
if (begin != -1) {
begin += cname.length;
end = dc.indexOf(";", begin);
if (end == -1) end = dc.length;
return unescape(dc.substring(begin, end));
}
}
return null;
}

//delete cookie
function eraseCookie (name,path,domain) {
if (getCookie(name)) {
document.cookie = name + "=" +
((path == null) ? "" : "; path=" + path) +
((domain == null) ? "" : "; domain=" + domain) +
"; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-70 00:00:01 GMT";
}
}

//]]&gt;
 </script>

              <h2 style="text-align: justify;">
               <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                Web Design BASIC TUTORIAL FOR BEGINNER PART-009
               </span>
              </h2>
              <div>
               <hr style="text-align: justify;"/>
               <h3 style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 Today I'll show you the use of HTML in the
                </span>
                <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0954356f-8312-448d-882e-ab026e61c200" id="ce79979e-1a2d-4d06-aa9d-54e4009e57fc" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0a71a06b-1776-4617-9138-2a40fcc46809" id="ba97db84-4308-430b-8932-ffbb57a8897f">
                  <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="cdcf8dc4-f700-4632-9092-47de118df973" id="2a2d5ccc-de24-44fb-9d30-c78301b79fe9">
                   <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="06339880-c807-4e73-a1ea-d5a3d3460dbb" id="dccfe71d-8a84-4e17-af7c-8862d39c088b">

                     iframe
                    </gs>
                   </gs>
                  </gs>
                 </gs>
                </gs>
                <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0954356f-8312-448d-882e-ab026e61c200" id="f4a98877-3cb7-466b-88e7-1bb227897b08" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0a71a06b-1776-4617-9138-2a40fcc46809" id="07989d79-857e-4d91-959d-caed57ff8c5c">

                   <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="06339880-c807-4e73-a1ea-d5a3d3460dbb" id="5eec1bf9-49ed-4af5-922d-19b3cc9bf48b">

                     ,
                    </gs>
                   </gs>
                  </gs>
                 </gs>
                </gs>
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 the colors and the colors and the layout of the code
                </span>
                <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0954356f-8312-448d-882e-ab026e61c200" id="2f7fb196-77a1-475a-a158-df6b7d82d1e3" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0a71a06b-1776-4617-9138-2a40fcc46809" id="468faa7d-06c8-4b96-b0c8-febd044c4f06">
                  <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="cdcf8dc4-f700-4632-9092-47de118df973" id="b6ee2c90-f30a-45e5-aa4f-2fbf600a37fc">
                   <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="06339880-c807-4e73-a1ea-d5a3d3460dbb" id="c2b29902-7c5b-4905-bc66-a49de1c17c38">
                    <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="eb2f1b25-2a49-45fb-93ff-cde51827914a" id="6423e017-e2d3-4432-b589-d768704e7f9b">
                     .
                    </gs>
                   </gs>
                  </gs>
                 </gs>
                </gs>
               </h3>
               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0954356f-8312-448d-882e-ab026e61c200" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="0a71a06b-1776-4617-9138-2a40fcc46809">

                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Grn7jMq3lOI/VUUZxHKZTzI/AAAAAAAAAyo/7TYUIzkHF-M/s1600/HTML.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                 <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Grn7jMq3lOI/VUUZxHKZTzI/AAAAAAAAAyo/7TYUIzkHF-M/s1600/HTML.png"/>

               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <br/>
               </div>
               <h3 style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="e698656b-e46a-4662-9b5c-2e662560ce81" id="3f3d9367-deba-4909-8d41-479681e00c1a">
                  <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="316b0d0e-be8a-49f4-9bc4-9b4585ff4bb8" id="a70fcdd8-795a-4e60-b899-3dc8f7900d13">
                   <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="95e4a828-f24d-45fb-8349-5c89378e86f5" id="1d804585-be01-4efe-8b46-e20c9e2fa976">
                    <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="73948020-bb8b-4aa5-a3c8-e344dba78e81" id="d769a43d-e56f-42d4-8768-f6303368dbd7">
                     <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="29e66799-7a92-49f4-857c-9efb3173d894" id="4a11489a-a99e-42de-bfbb-98f66ab98f88">
                      iframe
                     </gs>
                    </gs>
                   </gs>
                  </gs>
                 </gs>
                </span>
               </h3>
               <div style="text-align: justify;">
                <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                 Within a Web page to another Web page to display one or more of the way
                </span>
                <gs class="GINGER_SOFTWARE_mark" ginger_software_uiphraseguid="29f5f0f5-ba4b-4929-935b-ec82bd2f56da" id="1bcc173d-92a5-42bd-8889-0781c718b298" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">

   jQuery(document).ready(function($){
	var $ele = $('#BackToTop');
    $(window).scroll(function() {
        $(this).scrollTop() &gt;= 200 ? $ele.show(10).animate({ right : '15px' }, 10) : $ele.animate({ right : '-80px' }, 10);
    });
    $ele.click(function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('html,body').animate({
            scrollTop: 0
        }, 400);
    });
});

//Random Post
function showLucky(root){
    var feed = root.feed;
    var entries = feed.entry || [];
    var entry = feed.entry[0];
      for (var j = 0; j &lt; entry.link.length; ++j) {
       if (entry.link[j].rel == "alternate") { 
       window.location = entry.link[j].href; 
       } 
      } 
   }

function fetchLuck(luck){
    script = document.createElement('script');
    script.src = '/feeds/posts/summary?start-index='+luck+'&amp;max-results=1&amp;alt=json-in-script&amp;callback=showLucky';
    script.type = 'text/javascript';
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
   }
function readLucky(root){
    var feed = root.feed;
    var total = parseInt(feed.openSearch$totalResults.$t,10);
    var luckyNumber = Math.floor(Math.random()*total);
    luckyNumber++;
    fetchLuck(luckyNumber);
    }
function feelingLucky(){
    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.type = 'text/javascript';
    script.src = '/feeds/posts/summary?max-results=0&amp;alt=json-in-script&amp;callback=readLucky';
    document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
    }
//]]&gt;
  </script>

//Block Link Comments
function blockLinks(parentID, children) {
    var parent = document.getElementById(parentID),
        content = parent.getElementsByTagName(children);
    for(var i = 0; i &lt; content.length; i++) {
        if(content[i].innerHTML.indexOf('&lt;/a&gt;') !== -1) {
            content[i].innerHTML = "No more &lt;span style='background-color:rgba(255,255,255,0.3);color:#fff;padding:4px 8px;border-radius:3px'&gt;&lt;b&gt;live link&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt; in this comments field";
            content[i].className = "spammer-detected";
        }
    }
}
blockLinks('comment_block', 'p');

//Pre Comments Box
function cdClear() {
    var wtarea = document.getElementById('codes');
    wtarea.value = '';
    wtarea.focus();
    document.getElementById('cvrt').disabled = false;
}
function cdConvert() {
    var ctarea = document.getElementById('codes'),
        cv = ctarea.value,
        opt1 = document.getElementById('opt1'),
        opt2 = document.getElementById('opt2'),
        opt3 = document.getElementById('opt3'),
        opt4 = document.getElementById('opt4'),
        opt5 = document.getElementById('opt5');
    cv = cv.replace(/\t/g, "    ");
    if (opt1.checked) cv = cv.replace(/&amp;/g, "&amp;");
    if (opt2.checked) cv = cv.replace(/'/g, "&#039;");
    if (opt3.checked) cv = cv.replace(/"/g, "&quot;");
    if (opt4.checked) cv = cv.replace(/&lt;/g, "&lt;");
    if (opt5.checked) cv = cv.replace(/&gt;/g, "&gt;");
    if (cv.lastIndexOf('\n') != -1 || cv.length &gt; 40) {
        cv = cv.replace(/^/, "&lt;i rel=\"pre\"&gt;");
    } else {
        cv = cv.replace(/^/, "&lt;i rel=\"code\"&gt;");
    }
    cv = cv.replace(/$/, "&lt;/i&gt;");
    ctarea.value = cv;
    ctarea.focus();
    ctarea.select();
};
//]]&gt;
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[
var scrollTimer = null;
$(window).scroll(function() {
   var viewportHeight = $(this).height(),
       scrollbarHeight = viewportHeight / $(document).height() * viewportHeight,
       progress = $(this).scrollTop() / ($(document).height() - viewportHeight),
       distance = progress * (viewportHeight - scrollbarHeight) + scrollbarHeight / 2 - $('#scroll').height() / 2;
    $('#scroll')
        .css('top', distance)
        .text(' (' + Math.round(progress * 100) + '%)')
        .fadeIn(600);
    if (scrollTimer !== null) {
        clearTimeout(scrollTimer);
    }
    scrollTimer = setTimeout(function() {
        $('#scroll').fadeOut(600);
    }, 1000);
});
//]]&gt;
  </script>
